struct Array__Bool {
    own mut data : U8
    cap : U32
namespace:
    /// Create a zero-initialized Array with the given capacity.
    func new(shallow cap: U32) returns Array__Bool
    func len(self: Array__Bool) returns shallow U32
    /// Ref to the element at index `i`. Throws OutOfBounds if `i` is
    /// past the end; call as `arr.get(i)!` to panic on a bad index.
    func get(self: Array__Bool, i: U32, mut _err_kind: I64, mut _err_OutOfBounds: OutOfBounds) returns ref Bool
    /// Overwrite the element at index `i`. Drops the old value. `val` is
    /// owned. Throws OutOfBounds if `i` is past the end; call as
    /// `arr[i] = val` (or `arr.set(i, own val)!`) to panic on a bad index.
    func set(self: Array__Bool, shallow i: U32, own val: Bool, mut _err_kind: I64, mut _err_OutOfBounds: OutOfBounds)
    func delete(own self: Array__Bool, shallow call_free: Bool)
    func clone(self: Array__Bool) returns Array__Bool
    func size() returns shallow U32
}
#+end_src

** [[file:src/self/builder.org::*Map__Str_U32][Map__Str_U32]]
#+begin_src til
struct Map__Str_U32 {
    mut keys : Vec__Str
    mut values : Vec__U32
namespace:
    /// Create an empty Map of the types provided for the key and values respectively.
    /// The key type must implement `cmp`.
    func new() returns Map__Str_U32
    func len(self: Map__Str_U32) returns shallow U32
    /// Drop all live keys and values but keep the allocated storage so the Map can be reused.
    func clear(mut self: Map__Str_U32)
    /// Ref to the key slot at sorted index `i`. Unchecked: callers
    /// guarantee `i < self.keys.count` (Map's binary-search consumers
    /// always validate before calling). Bypasses Vec.get's throwing
    /// bounds check.
    func key_ptr(self: Map__Str_U32, i: U32) returns ref Str
    /// Ref to the value slot at sorted index `i`. Same caller-validated
    /// contract as key_ptr.
    func val_ptr(self: Map__Str_U32, i: U32) returns ref U32
    /// True if a value exists for the given key.
    func has(self: Map__Str_U32, key: Str) returns shallow Bool
    /// Return a ref to the value for `key`. Throws KeyNotFound if
    /// `key` is absent; call as `map.get(k)!` (or `map[k]`) to panic
    /// on a missing key.
    func get(self: Map__Str_U32, key: Str, mut _err_kind: I64, mut _err_KeyNotFound: KeyNotFound) returns ref U32
    /// Insert or overwrite the value for `key`. The value is owned.
    func set(mut self: Map__Str_U32, key: Str, own val: U32)
    func delete(own self: Map__Str_U32, shallow call_free: Bool)
    func clone(self: Map__Str_U32) returns Map__Str_U32
    func hash(self: Map__Str_U32, hasher: HashFn) returns shallow U64
    func size() returns shallow U32
}
#+end_src

** [[file:src/self/builder.org::*Vec__DynCallInfo][Vec__DynCallInfo]]
#+begin_src til
struct Vec__DynCallInfo {
    own mut data : U8
    mut count : U32
    mut cap : U32
namespace:
    /// Create a new empty Vec for elements of type T.
    func new() returns Vec__DynCallInfo
    func len(self: Vec__DynCallInfo) returns shallow U32
    /// Drop all live elements via elem_delete but keep the allocated
    /// storage and element-type metadata so the Vec can be reused.
    func clear(mut self: Vec__DynCallInfo)
    /// Append an element to the end. `val` is owned: after this call the
    /// caller must not use the value passed -- clone it first if needed.
    func push(mut self: Vec__DynCallInfo, own val: priv___src_self_builder_til__DynCallInfo)
    /// Consume the contents of `other` by appending them to `self`.
    /// `other` is taken by ownership and will be empty after the call.
    func append(mut self: Vec__DynCallInfo, own other: Vec__DynCallInfo)
    /// Replace self's contents with other's via memcpy (no per-elem clone).
    /// Avoids the Vec_clone + extra Vec_delete that plain `self = other` emits.
    /// Takes `mut` (not `own`) so caller retains ownership of other; its
    /// natural scope-end auto-delete frees other.data. Setting other.count = 0
    /// prevents that auto-delete from re-running elem_delete on items whose
    /// bytes were moved into self.
    func move_from(mut self: Vec__DynCallInfo, mut other: Vec__DynCallInfo)
    /// Return a reference to the element at index `i`. Throws
    /// OutOfBounds if `i` is past the end; call as `vec[i]`
    /// to panic on a bad index. The reference is valid until the
    /// next mutation.
    func get(self: Vec__DynCallInfo, i: U32, mut _err_kind: I64, mut _err_OutOfBounds: OutOfBounds) returns ref priv___src_self_builder_til__DynCallInfo
    /// Remove and return the last element. Panics if empty. The caller
    /// takes ownership of the returned value.
    func pop(mut self: Vec__DynCallInfo) returns priv___src_self_builder_til__DynCallInfo
    /// Split off the first `n` elements into a new Vec. Panics if `n`
    /// exceeds self.len(). The remaining elements shift to the front.
    func take_prefix(mut self: Vec__DynCallInfo, shallow n: U32) returns Vec__DynCallInfo
    /// Overwrite the element at index `i`. `val` is owned. Throws
    /// OutOfBounds if `i` is past the end; call as `vec[i] = val`
    /// (or `vec.set(i, own val)!`) to panic on a bad index.
    func set(mut self: Vec__DynCallInfo, shallow i: U32, own val: priv___src_self_builder_til__DynCallInfo, mut _err_kind: I64, mut _err_OutOfBounds: OutOfBounds)
    /// Move bytes of src[i] into self (push). Source slot is zeroed so that
    /// src's eventual elem_delete on it is a no-op (relies on the same
    /// count==0/data==NULL convention used by take_children and Vec.delete).
    func push_take(mut self: Vec__DynCallInfo, mut src: Vec__DynCallInfo, shallow i: U32)
    /// Drop each element via elem_delete, free storage, then free self
    /// unless `call_free` is false.
    func delete(own self: Vec__DynCallInfo, shallow call_free: Bool)
    /// Deep-copy the Vec and all its elements via elem_clone.
    func clone(self: Vec__DynCallInfo) returns Vec__DynCallInfo
    func size() returns shallow U32
}
#+end_src

** [[file:vendor/bindings/libffi.org::*ffi_closure][ffi_closure]]

struct ffi_closure {
namespace:
    func clone(_self: ffi_closure) returns ffi_closure
    func delete(own self: ffi_closure, shallow call_free: Bool)
    func hash(self: ffi_closure, hasher: HashFn) returns shallow U64
    func eq(_self: ffi_closure, _other: ffi_closure) returns shallow Bool
    func to_str(_self: ffi_closure) returns Str
    func size() returns shallow U32
}

** [[file:src/self/interpreter.org::*Map__Str_Binding][Map__Str_Binding]]
#+begin_src til
struct Map__Str_Binding {
    mut keys : Vec__Str
    mut values : Vec__Binding
namespace:
    /// Create an empty Map of the types provided for the key and values respectively.
    /// The key type must implement `cmp`.
    func new() returns Map__Str_Binding
    func len(self: Map__Str_Binding) returns shallow U32
    /// Drop all live keys and values but keep the allocated storage so the Map can be reused.
    func clear(mut self: Map__Str_Binding)
    /// Ref to the key slot at sorted index `i`. Unchecked: callers
    /// guarantee `i < self.keys.count` (Map's binary-search consumers
    /// always validate before calling). Bypasses Vec.get's throwing
    /// bounds check.
    func key_ptr(self: Map__Str_Binding, i: U32) returns ref Str
    /// Ref to the value slot at sorted index `i`. Same caller-validated
    /// contract as key_ptr.
    func val_ptr(self: Map__Str_Binding, i: U32) returns ref Binding
    /// True if a value exists for the given key.
    func has(self: Map__Str_Binding, key: Str) returns shallow Bool
    /// Return a ref to the value for `key`. Throws KeyNotFound if
    /// `key` is absent; call as `map.get(k)!` (or `map[k]`) to panic
    /// on a missing key.
    func get(self: Map__Str_Binding, key: Str, mut _err_kind: I64, mut _err_KeyNotFound: KeyNotFound) returns ref Binding
    /// Insert or overwrite the value for `key`. The value is owned.
    func set(mut self: Map__Str_Binding, key: Str, own val: Binding)
    func delete(own self: Map__Str_Binding, shallow call_free: Bool)
    func clone(self: Map__Str_Binding) returns Map__Str_Binding
    func hash(self: Map__Str_Binding, hasher: HashFn) returns shallow U64
    func size() returns shallow U32
}
#+end_src

** [[file:src/self/interpreter.org::*Vec__DynPtrBox][Vec__DynPtrBox]]
#+begin_src til
struct Vec__DynPtrBox {
    own mut data : U8
    mut count : U32
    mut cap : U32
namespace:
    /// Create a new empty Vec for elements of type T.
    func new() returns Vec__DynPtrBox
    func len(self: Vec__DynPtrBox) returns shallow U32
    /// Drop all live elements via elem_delete but keep the allocated
    /// storage and element-type metadata so the Vec can be reused.
    func clear(mut self: Vec__DynPtrBox)
    /// Append an element to the end. `val` is owned: after this call the
    /// caller must not use the value passed -- clone it first if needed.
    func push(mut self: Vec__DynPtrBox, own val: priv___src_self_interpreter_til__DynPtrBox)
    /// Consume the contents of `other` by appending them to `self`.
    /// `other` is taken by ownership and will be empty after the call.
    func append(mut self: Vec__DynPtrBox, own other: Vec__DynPtrBox)
    /// Replace self's contents with other's via memcpy (no per-elem clone).
    /// Avoids the Vec_clone + extra Vec_delete that plain `self = other` emits.
    /// Takes `mut` (not `own`) so caller retains ownership of other; its
    /// natural scope-end auto-delete frees other.data. Setting other.count = 0
    /// prevents that auto-delete from re-running elem_delete on items whose
    /// bytes were moved into self.
    func move_from(mut self: Vec__DynPtrBox, mut other: Vec__DynPtrBox)
    /// Return a reference to the element at index `i`. Throws
    /// OutOfBounds if `i` is past the end; call as `vec[i]`
    /// to panic on a bad index. The reference is valid until the
    /// next mutation.
    func get(self: Vec__DynPtrBox, i: U32, mut _err_kind: I64, mut _err_OutOfBounds: OutOfBounds) returns ref priv___src_self_interpreter_til__DynPtrBox
    /// Remove and return the last element. Panics if empty. The caller
    /// takes ownership of the returned value.
    func pop(mut self: Vec__DynPtrBox) returns priv___src_self_interpreter_til__DynPtrBox
    /// Split off the first `n` elements into a new Vec. Panics if `n`
    /// exceeds self.len(). The remaining elements shift to the front.
    func take_prefix(mut self: Vec__DynPtrBox, shallow n: U32) returns Vec__DynPtrBox
    /// Overwrite the element at index `i`. `val` is owned. Throws
    /// OutOfBounds if `i` is past the end; call as `vec[i] = val`
    /// (or `vec.set(i, own val)!`) to panic on a bad index.
    func set(mut self: Vec__DynPtrBox, shallow i: U32, own val: priv___src_self_interpreter_til__DynPtrBox, mut _err_kind: I64, mut _err_OutOfBounds: OutOfBounds)
    /// Move bytes of src[i] into self (push). Source slot is zeroed so that
    /// src's eventual elem_delete on it is a no-op (relies on the same
    /// count==0/data==NULL convention used by take_children and Vec.delete).
    func push_take(mut self: Vec__DynPtrBox, mut src: Vec__DynPtrBox, shallow i: U32)
    /// Drop each element via elem_delete, free storage, then free self
    /// unless `call_free` is false.
    func delete(own self: Vec__DynPtrBox, shallow call_free: Bool)
    /// Deep-copy the Vec and all its elements via elem_clone.
    func clone(self: Vec__DynPtrBox) returns Vec__DynPtrBox
    func size() returns shallow U32
}
#+end_src

** [[file:src/self/interpreter.org::*Vec__Binding][Vec__Binding]]
#+begin_src til
struct Vec__Binding {
    own mut data : U8
    mut count : U32
    mut cap : U32
namespace:
    /// Create a new empty Vec for elements of type T.
    func new() returns Vec__Binding
    func len(self: Vec__Binding) returns shallow U32
    /// Drop all live elements via elem_delete but keep the allocated
    /// storage and element-type metadata so the Vec can be reused.
    func clear(mut self: Vec__Binding)
    /// Append an element to the end. `val` is owned: after this call the
    /// caller must not use the value passed -- clone it first if needed.
    func push(mut self: Vec__Binding, own val: Binding)
    /// Consume the contents of `other` by appending them to `self`.
    /// `other` is taken by ownership and will be empty after the call.
    func append(mut self: Vec__Binding, own other: Vec__Binding)
    /// Replace self's contents with other's via memcpy (no per-elem clone).
    /// Avoids the Vec_clone + extra Vec_delete that plain `self = other` emits.
    /// Takes `mut` (not `own`) so caller retains ownership of other; its
    /// natural scope-end auto-delete frees other.data. Setting other.count = 0
    /// prevents that auto-delete from re-running elem_delete on items whose
    /// bytes were moved into self.
    func move_from(mut self: Vec__Binding, mut other: Vec__Binding)
    /// Return a reference to the element at index `i`. Throws
    /// OutOfBounds if `i` is past the end; call as `vec[i]`
    /// to panic on a bad index. The reference is valid until the
    /// next mutation.
    func get(self: Vec__Binding, i: U32, mut _err_kind: I64, mut _err_OutOfBounds: OutOfBounds) returns ref Binding
    /// Remove and return the last element. Panics if empty. The caller
    /// takes ownership of the returned value.
    func pop(mut self: Vec__Binding) returns Binding
    /// Split off the first `n` elements into a new Vec. Panics if `n`
    /// exceeds self.len(). The remaining elements shift to the front.
    func take_prefix(mut self: Vec__Binding, shallow n: U32) returns Vec__Binding
    /// Overwrite the element at index `i`. `val` is owned. Throws
    /// OutOfBounds if `i` is past the end; call as `vec[i] = val`
    /// (or `vec.set(i, own val)!`) to panic on a bad index.
    func set(mut self: Vec__Binding, shallow i: U32, own val: Binding, mut _err_kind: I64, mut _err_OutOfBounds: OutOfBounds)
    /// Move bytes of src[i] into self (push). Source slot is zeroed so that
    /// src's eventual elem_delete on it is a no-op (relies on the same
    /// count==0/data==NULL convention used by take_children and Vec.delete).
    func push_take(mut self: Vec__Binding, mut src: Vec__Binding, shallow i: U32)
    /// Drop each element via elem_delete, free storage, then free self
    /// unless `call_free` is false.
    func delete(own self: Vec__Binding, shallow call_free: Bool)
    /// Deep-copy the Vec and all its elements via elem_clone.
    func clone(self: Vec__Binding) returns Vec__Binding
    func size() returns shallow U32

#+begin_src til
struct nng_url {
    ref mut u_rawurl : I8
    ref mut u_scheme : I8
    ref mut u_userinfo : I8
    ref mut u_host : I8
    ref mut u_hostname : I8
    ref mut u_port : I8
    ref mut u_path : I8
    ref mut u_query : I8
    ref mut u_fragment : I8
    ref mut u_requri : I8
namespace:
    func clone(self: nng_url) returns nng_url
    func delete(own self: nng_url, shallow call_free: Bool)
    func size() returns shallow U32
}

** [[file:vendor/bindings/nng.org::*nng_udp][nng_udp]]
#+begin_src til
struct nng_udp {
namespace:
    func clone(_self: nng_udp) returns nng_udp
    func delete(own self: nng_udp, shallow call_free: Bool)
    func hash(self: nng_udp, hasher: HashFn) returns shallow U64
    func eq(_self: nng_udp, _other: nng_udp) returns shallow Bool
    func to_str(_self: nng_udp) returns Str
    func size() returns shallow U32
}
#+end_src

** [[file:src/til.org::*CliArgs][CliArgs]]
#+begin_src til
struct CliArgs {
    mut command : Str
    mut path : Str
    mut custom_bin : Str
    mut custom_c : Str
    mut target_str : Str
    mut cc : Str
    mut install_prefix : Str
    mut path_idx : U32
    mut early_return : Bool
    mut asan : Bool
    mut prof : Bool
    own mut extra_modes
namespace:
    func clone(self: CliArgs) returns CliArgs
    func delete(own self: CliArgs, shallow call_free: Bool)
    func size() returns shallow U32
}
#+end_src
